  tale, talk\\%

  \hspace*{\fill}\rule[0pt]{0.2\cardinnerwidth}{0.5pt}\hspace*{\fill}%

\item はなす\\*
to talk, to speak, to converse
\item はなし\\*
talk, speech, chat
\item でんわ\\*

\item わだい\\*
topic, subject
\item はなしあう\\*

\item たいわ\\*

  \end{multicols}%
